## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: nonlinear oscillator dynamics
**Analysis**: This task involves finding the acceleration (dv/dt) of a nonlinear harmonic oscillator as a function of position, velocity, and time. The acceleration is governed by restoring forces (functions of x) and damping forces (functions of v), possibly with nonlinear terms like cubic restoring forces (Duffing oscillator) or nonlinear damping.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- Simple harmonic restoring force: dv_dt = c0 * x (linear restoring force)
- Damped harmonic oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v (linear restoring + linear damping)
- Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 (cubic nonlinear restoring force)
- Damped Duffing oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v (cubic restoring + damping)
- Van der Pol oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * (1 - x**2) * v (nonlinear damping)
- Quintic nonlinear oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * x**5 (higher-order restoring force)
- Nonlinear damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v * abs(v) (quadratic velocity damping)
- Cubic damping: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * v + c2 * v**3 (nonlinear velocity-dependent damping)
- Forced Duffing: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**3 + c2 * v + c3 * sin(c4 * t) (driven nonlinear oscillator)
- Parametric oscillator: dv_dt = c0 * x * cos(c1 * t) (time-modulated stiffness)
- Mixed nonlinearity: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 + c2 * x**3 (asymmetric + symmetric nonlinearity)
- Position-velocity coupling: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x * v (multiplicative coupling term)
- General polynomial restoring: dv_dt = c0 * x + c1 * x**2 + c2 * x**3 + c3 * v (polynomial potential with damping)
- Softening/hardening spring: dv_dt = c0 * x * (1 + c1 * x**2) (amplitude-dependent stiffness)

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope → Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects → Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay → Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior → Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects → Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Odd-power restoring forces (x, x**3, x**5) → symmetric potential wells preserving oscillation symmetry
- Even-power terms in position (x**2) → asymmetric potential indicating broken symmetry in the restoring force
- Velocity-dependent terms proportional to v → linear energy dissipation or injection (damping/driving)
- Terms like (1 - x**2)*v → amplitude-dependent damping characteristic of self-sustained oscillations (limit cycles)
- Cubic position terms x**3 → Duffing-type hardening (positive coefficient) or softening (negative coefficient) spring behavior
- Sinusoidal time dependence sin(c*t) or cos(c*t) → external periodic driving force leading to resonance phenomena
- Product terms x*v → nonlinear energy exchange between kinetic and potential degrees of freedom
- Absence of explicit time dependence → autonomous system where phase portrait fully characterizes dynamics
- Higher odd powers of velocity (v**3) → nonlinear drag forces common in fluid-structure interaction

I need to determine which candidates are equivalent to the ground truth:

**GT: F0*sin(t) - beta*exp(-|x|)*v = 0.156063*sin(t) - 0.372948*v*exp(-x)**

Since x > 0 on this domain, |x| = x, so GT = c_a*sin(t) + c_b*v*exp(-x).

The GT has two basis functions: **sin(t)** and **v*exp(-x)**.

Let me check each candidate for whether it can express exactly this form.

**Candidate 1:** `(c0*v + c1 + (c2*v + c3*sin(c4 + t))*(c5*x + c6))/(c5*x + c6)`
= c0*v/(c5*x + c6) + c1/(c5*x + c6) + c2*v + c3*sin(c4 + t)
This has v/(linear in x) and 1/(linear in x) terms that can't produce v*exp(-x). Setting c0=c1=0 gives c2*v + c3*sin(c4+t), which is linear in v, not v*exp(-x).
Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 2:** `c0*v + c1*sin(c2 + t) + c3*v*x**c4`
= (c0 + c3*x^c4)*v + c1*sin(c2+t). The v-coefficient is c0 + c3*x^c4, a power law in x. exp(-x) is not a power law.
Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 3:** `c0*sin(c1 + t) + c2*v*exp(c3*x)`
With c1=0, c3=-1: c0*sin(t) + c2*v*exp(-x). This matches GT exactly!
Candidate 3 verdict: [MATCH]

**Candidate 4:** `c0*sin(t) + c1*v*(x²-1) + c2*v*(c3+x)^c4`
v*(x²-1) is polynomial, v*(c3+x)^c4 is power law. Sum of these can't equal v*exp(-x).
Candidate 4 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 5:** `c0*v + c1*sin(t) + c2*v*(c3+x)^c4`
= (c0 + c2*(c3+x)^c4)*v + c1*sin(t). Power law ≠ exp(-x).
Candidate 5 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 6:** `c0*v*(x²-1) + c1*sin(t) + c2*v*x^c3`
Polynomial + power law in x times v ≠ v*exp(-x).

With c2=-1: c0*sin(t) + c1*v*exp(-x). Matches GT!
